Our processing of Personal Data on behalf of Customers, as Data Processor, is regulated by the Data Processing Agreement entered into upon the Customer’s use of the Services. See also section 3 of this Privacy Policy.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">1.3</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Protecting your Personal Data is our highest priority regardless of whether such Personal Data relates your use of our Services, website or other correspondence between you and the Company. transition-duration: 0.5s;">2.3</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">“Data Controller” and “Data Processor” shall mean “controller” and “processor” respectively as defined in the GDPR.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-duration: 0.5s;">“Personal Data” shall mean any information relating to an identified or identifiable natural person (‘data subject’); an identifiable natural person is one who can be identified, directly or indirectly, in particular by reference to an identifier such as a name, an identification number, location data, an online identifier or to one or more factors specific to the physical, physiological, genetic, mental, economic, cultural or social identity of that natural person.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">3.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">This Privacy Policy describes our processing of Personal Data as Data Controller of Personal Data connected to the Customer’s subscription to our Services or trial period. With respect to all Personal Data entered, transferred or stored on behalf of the Customers in the databases of the Company or a third-party supplier appointed by the Company, the Customer is the Data Controller and the Company is the Data Processor.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">3.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Our processing of Personal Data on behalf of the Customer is regulated by the Data Processing Agreement, which is entered into upon the Customer’s subscription to the Services or a free trial period.</p><h1 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;" class="preFlex"><strong>4 CATEGORIES OF PERSONAL DATA</strong></h1><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">4.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Personal Data includes information that can be used to identify you as an individual. If you sign up to our Services or a free trial, we might ask you to provide us with certain personal identifiable information that can be used to identify you, including:</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">a)</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Contact information, such as email address, telephone number first and last name</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">b)</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Username(s) of authorised users and IP address</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">c)</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Information collected via <a href="https://www.meetinvr.com/">www.completion.</a>one, including cookies and usage data (see section 10).</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">d)</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Additionally, when using the VR app some information is required to be processed for the basic functionality of the app and in some cases be stored. This information includes, but is not limited to, voice data and VR/AR tracking data.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">4.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Voice data.</span> When using the VR App, your voice data is transferred and processed through our secure servers with a secure connection for the purposes of voice communication with other users. Voice communication may be disabled in the app. In some cases, voice data may be recorded if requested by the user and will be explicitly indicated by the app. Voice recording are only stored securely in our databases and is only available to the user.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">4.3</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">VR/AR tracking data.</span> To use the VR app positional data is required to position and pose your avatar in the virtual space. Tracking data is only transferred and processed through our secure servers with a secure connection. The data may be recorded when requested by you similarly to your voice data. Positional and voice data may be stored and processed together in some cases.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">4.4</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">As the clear main rule, we do not collect or process any sensitive Personal Data.</p><h1 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">6.3</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">We will take all steps reasonably necessary to ensure that your data is treated securely and in accordance with this Privacy Policy and no transfer of your Personal Data will take place to an organization or a country unless there are adequate controls in place including the security of your Personal Data and other information.</p><h1 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;" class="preFlex"><strong>7 OUR USE OF DATA PROCESSORS</strong></h1><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">7.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); The storage (or retention) period depends on the nature of the information and the background for storage. It is therefore not possible to specify a specific time frame for deletion of Personal Data in each case in this Privacy Policy. However, we have described our general retention rules in section 9.2 below.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">8.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Generally, we process Personal Data about Customers for a period of up to three (3) years from effective termination of the Customer’s use of our Services. However, Personal Data related to payments must be kept for five (5) years + the current calendar year after the end of the accounting year according to Danish rules on bookkeeping. Personal Data may be stored for a longer period if the Personal Data is needed to establish, exercise or defend a legal claim</p><h1 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;" class="preFlex"><strong>9 SECURITY MEASURES</strong></h1><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">9.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">We have taken technical and organizational measures to prevent your information from being accidentally or illegally deleted, disclosed, lost, impaired, misused or otherwise violated by law.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">9.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">We use encryption of data which means that all data transmitted between your device and our servers is unreadable to outsiders. To access your account, you need your personal username and password and must go through our authentication process. All data is transmitted using secure protocols, such as HTTPS and WSS. We do not knowingly allow any unencrypted data to be exposed. All data is encrypted at rest at an underlying level. Extra sensitive information, such as login credentials have additional encryption at the application level. Very little data is stored on the user’s physical device, and only include low-risk information such as parameters used to display the user’s avatar.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">9.3</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">We host all data on up-to-date Google cluster servers that are protected against unauthorized access by a firewall. Some data and backups are stored with Google Cloud Storage</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">9.4</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">We have internal rules on information security and annual training session for all employees about best practices to secure themselves and the Company’s Personal Data. Our internal rules on information security contain instructions and measures to protect Personal Data from being destroyed, lost or modified, from unauthorized disclosure, and against unauthorized access or knowledge of them. We will ensure that collected Personal Data are treated with care and protected according to applicable safety standards. We have strict security procedures for collecting, storing and transferring Personal Data to prevent unauthorized access.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">9.5</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">The security of your Personal Data is very important to us, but remember that no online transmissions, or method of electronic storage is 100% secure. While we strive to use commercially validated means to protect your Personal Data, we cannot guarantee its absolute security.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">9.6</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">We assess the risk of our processing of Personal Data on an ongoing basis. You can see the most commonly asked questions and answers to our Information Security measures in our FAQ available through <a href="https://www.meetinvr.com/">www.completion.</a>one.</p><h1 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;" class="preFlex"><strong>10 COOKIES</strong></h1><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">We use cookies and similar tracking technologies to track the activity on our website and IT tool. Cookies are files with small amount of data which may include an anonymous unique identifier. Cookies are sent to your browser from our website and stored on your device. Tracking technologies also used are beacons, tags, and scripts to collect and track information.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">You can instruct your browser to refuse all cookies or to indicate when a cookie is being sent. However, if you do not accept cookies, you may not be able to use some portions of our website.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.3</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Consent to use of cookies</span></p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.3.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">When visiting our website <a href="https://www.meetinvr.com/">www.completion.</a>one, you will be asked for your consent to the cookies used on the website (technically necessary cookies are applied automatically). If you have consented to the website’s use of cookies, but no longer wish to consent to the use of cookies, you can deselect and delete the cookies by modifying the settings in your browser (see section 10.8 on “Deletion of cookies”).</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.4</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Types of cookies</span></p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.4.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Session cookies and persistent cookies.</span>There are two types of cookies – session cookies and persistent cookies. Session cookies are bits of information that are erased when you close your web browser. Persistent cookies are bits of information that are stored on your computer until they are erased. Persistent cookies erase themselves after a certain period of time but are renewed each time you visit <a href="https://www.meetinvr.com/">www.completion.</a>one. Our website uses both session cookies and persistent cookies.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.4.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">“Own” cookies and third-party cookies.</span> Cookies can be placed on <a href="https://www.meetinvr.com/">www.completion.</a>one by the Company itself or by third parties such as Google or Meta (see below for information about the use of Google Analytics).</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.5</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Purposes</span></p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.5.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Session cookies.</span> We use session cookies to operate this website and our IT tool.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.5.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Persistent cookies.</span> We use persistent cookies to remember your preferences and various settings and security cookies for security purposes. We also use persistent cookies for marketing purposes, such as Google Ads Remarketing (only with your consent).</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.6</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Google Analytics</span></p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.6.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">We use Google Analytics. Google Analytics is a web analytics service offered by Google that tracks and reports website traffic. Google uses the data collected to track and monitor the use of our website. This data is shared with other Google services. Google may use the collected data to contextualize and personalize the ads of its own advertising network.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.7</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Social media.</span> We use social media buttons to allow you to connect with your social network. For these to work the following social media sites Facebook, Discord, Instagram and Twitter, will set cookies through our site which may be used to enhance your profile on their site or contribute to the data they hold for various purposes outlined in their respective privacy policies.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.8</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Deletion of cookies</span></p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.8.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Most browsers allow you to erase cookies from your hard drive via the browser settings, block all cookies or receive a warning before a cookie is stored. You must be aware that in such case services and features cannot be used by you because they require cookies to remember choices you make.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.8.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">You can opt-out of having made your activity on the service available to Google Analytics by installing the Google Analytics opt-out browser add-on. The add-on prevents the Google Analytics JavaScript (ga.js, analytics.js, and dc.js) from sharing information with Google Analytics about visits activity. For more information on the privacy practices of Google, please visit the Google Privacy &amp; Terms web page.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.9</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Links to other websites</span></p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.9.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Our website may contain links to other sites that are not operated by the Company. We strongly advise you to review the privacy policy of every site you visit</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">10.9.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;" class="preFlex"><strong>11 YOUR RIGHTS</strong></h1><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">You have certain rights related to our processing of your Personal Data according to the GDPR.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">In short, your rights include (see also Articles 15-22 in the GDPR):</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.2.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><strong>Right of access.</strong> You are entitled to be informed whether any Personal Data about the subject is being processed and if so, obtain access to the Personal Data.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.2.2</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><strong>Right of data portability.</strong> You are entitled to receive Personal Data that you have provided to The Company (this data must be provided in a structured, commonly used and machine-readable format).</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.2.3</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><strong>Right to rectification.</strong> You are entitled to obtain rectification of incorrect Personal Data.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.2.4</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><strong>Right of deletion.</strong> You are (with certain limitations), entitled to request erasure of Personal Data by us without undue delay.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.2.5</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><strong>Right to object.</strong> You are entitled to object to the processing of your personal data, namely if the processing of your personal data includes profiling or if the processing is based on the assessment of our interest in processing your personal data)</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.2.6</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;"><strong>Right to restriction of processing.</strong> You are entitled to obtain a restriction of the processing of your personal data, namely if you contest the accuracy of the personal data, or where a request to be deleted cannot be accommodated, e.g. due to The Company’ need to keep the personal data for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.3</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Please note that the above-mentioned rights will only be individually fulfilled by The Company in relation to the cases where The Company is considered as the Data Controller. In situations where The Company is regarded as the data processor, the above-mentioned rights must be fulfilled by the data controller.</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">11.4</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">Inquiries related to your rights according to GDPR can be made to: info@completion.one.</p><h1 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;" class="preFlex"><strong>12 CHANGES TO THIS PRIVACY POLICY</strong></h1><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">12.1</p><p class="preFlex" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.19, 1, 0.22, 1); transition-duration: 0.5s;">We may update this Privacy Policy.             sectionBackground.style.top = headerHeight + 'px';
          } else {
            sectionBackground.style.top = '';
          }
